  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
    background: var(--chops-white);
    border-radius: 6px;
    --chops-button-padding: 0.25em 8px;
    margin: 0;
    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);

  .input-grid {

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





I found that by changing the PoC a little, it is indeed possible to reproduce 



<span class="line"><!---->I found that by changing the PoC a little, it is indeed possible to reproduce <!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1404001



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1404001"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1404001<!----></a>





 on Android.



<span class="line"><!----> on Android.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





On Android, there are two types of installation prompts for PWAs



<span class="line"><!---->On Android, there are two types of installation prompts for PWAs<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





(1) Installation prompt with description and screenshot fields. This causes a popup from the bottom. This can be seen in 



<span class="line"><!---->(1) Installation prompt with description and screenshot fields. This causes a popup from the bottom. This can be seen in <!----></span>





https://coordinated-tartan-individual.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://coordinated-tartan-individual.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://coordinated-tartan-individual.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





(2) Installation prompt without description and screenshot fields. This causes a box to be drawn in the middle. This can be seen in 



<span class="line"><!---->(2) Installation prompt without description and screenshot fields. This causes a box to be drawn in the middle. This can be seen in <!----></span>





https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The installation prompt for (1) will disappear on Android when it navigates to other origins - ref: 



<span class="line"><!---->The installation prompt for (1) will disappear on Android when it navigates to other origins - ref: <!----></span>





https://jewel-chip-panama.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://jewel-chip-panama.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://jewel-chip-panama.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>





 On the other hand, the installation prompt for (2) will NOT disappear when Android navigates to other origins.



<span class="line"><!----> On the other hand, the installation prompt for (2) will NOT disappear when Android navigates to other origins.<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: [108.0.5359.128]<!----></span>

Operating System: [Android 11]



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: [Android 11]<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. On Android, go to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. On Android, go to <!----></span>





https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://shade-cactus-dragon.glitch.me/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





2. Press when tick appears. The prompt appears and Android will navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->2. Press when tick appears. The prompt appears and Android will navigate to <!----></span>





https://microsoft.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://microsoft.com"><!---->https://microsoft.com<!----></a>





 at the same time.



<span class="line"><!----> at the same time.<!----></span>

Forgot to mention the security implication of downloading a malicious PWA:



<span class="line"><!---->Forgot to mention the security implication of downloading a malicious PWA:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The security implication is that a user who is tricked into installing a PWA may be convinced that they have downloaded the real "Microsoft Teams" app / PWA. This can  lead to phishing of the user as the user thinks that the PWA is the real Microsoft Teams app and the PWA lacks any omnibox.



<span class="line"><!---->The security implication is that a user who is tricked into installing a PWA may be convinced that they have downloaded the real "Microsoft Teams" app / PWA. This can  lead to phishing of the user as the user thinks that the PWA is the real Microsoft Teams app and the PWA lacks any omnibox.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
